Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant; et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos; et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule; et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	Of these one method is that you make three or four cauterizations along the length of the mouse, according to the figure of the liver cauterization as we have said before; and do not press your hand over the entire cautery area, and let the patient lie on his back with their stomach up; and another method of cauterization is that you heat a cautery with two sides, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder; and lift the side where the mouse is, or where the pain of the patient comes from left to right, and let the elevations by which you lift the side be along the rib according to the length of the body, and the cauterization should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	After placing the two nerves inflamed until the pain is felt on the other side, and then draw out the cautery, and thus there will be four [stages]. And if you wish, cauterize the entire area with three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when pus has been discharged for a long time, it is worth noting that this happens more than with the other treatments mentioned before.
de ydropisie	of hydropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cautery is not effective for one suffering from hydropsy, except in the manner called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat it according to the methods we have described in divisions, and your treatment is ineffective, then you must apply four cauteries around the navel, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the spleen, two behind the spine, and one near the kidney; and let the cauteries be close to the area of pain.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After leaving the cautery open to discharge pus for a long time, and do not leave the treatment of the patient after the cautery; and healing would be hastened, and both intentions would come together with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the cautery for the abdomen should be the cleaver that we have shown before; and that for the back should be olive-shaped, as it is placed above.
de l’enfleure des piez	for swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the feet are swollen in one who is suffering from dropsy and are filled with yellow water, you must cauterize on the back of the foot between the little finger and the ring finger; and lift your hand with the cautery as you turn.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, thus you might miss the correct spot, and apply the cautery according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After make on each leg two cauterizations at the tip of the kneecap; and let the cauterizations be long, one below the knee in front and the other outside, in the middle of the leg; and leave the cauterizations uncovered for a while without cleaning, so that it takes effect; then cure according to the other methods we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When relief of the abdomen comes from cold and moisture, to such an extent that the retentive and digestive virtues in the stomach and intestines are weakened, and cannot be cured by usual methods; and you see the patient suffering greatly with great strength, then make a large cautery on the stomach as previously described for the fire cautery of the stomach, a circular cautery; and four small cauterizations around the navel, all together one small clavicle-shaped cautery, and two cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the patient suffering from abundant moisture, perform cauterization on the wrist, and one cauterization on each nodule, and two small cauterizations near the stomach around the large area, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the hemorrhoids are in the anus, whether one or more, and they are old, made of large cold and moist corrupted humors, and have been treated as we said in divisions, but it does not help, then perform cauterizations: three on the spine of the back, those which are farthest out behind each buttock forming a triangle, and one cauterization below the navel two fingers away; and if you think that their stomach is cooled off, and the food does not cook, and swelling in the face is seen, then on the face perform one large cauterization above the stomach as previously described, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen for the entire clavicle cautery; and leave the cauterization open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treating the area until it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the flesh condition which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you cut into the thelul, heat the cautery until it looks like a razor, and then place the burning cautery on the cut thelul; leave your hand there until the cautery reaches the base of the vein, from which blood will flow; do this once or twice, and if there is much thelul, cauterize each area as we have said; afterward, treat with beneficial ointments until it is healed; and if you cauterize a large area on the flesh with one cautery, it will provide greater benefit.
de plaie mal curee	of an improperly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure cutting or opening, which we will recount in its place, such a disease comes that cannot be healed except by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When a fistula comes to someone and is inflamed and discharges corrupt moisture and pus, then you should apply a fine poultice at once, and be sure that the poultice is of proper depth.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After heating the cautery which resembles a razor, apply it to the fistula according to how deep the poultice has gone in, and continue with the cautery until all the pus-filled and corrupted tissue is burned up, once or twice or three times as needed; but be careful not to burn the nerves that are nearby and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula goes to the bladder and intestines, be careful in these places, and do not make it open except where there is flesh, and think that it is not healing properly; afterwards treat the place until it is healed, and if the place is swollen and the matter has been removed for a long time, then know that the place is completely healed; and if the matter is not removed, know that the place is trapped, and the bone is corrupted; and thus as one of those we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the illness of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When pain from cold comes to the kidneys, and there is great gas formation, and it does not respond to female treatment, then you must make a cautery on the kidneys from one side and the other with the clavicle cautere that we mentioned before; and if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauters in a line, and they will provide greater help.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is weak and cold from coldness and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then you apply a cautery on the outer part above the bladder, where the hairs of the pubis begin, one on each side, and each cautery should be as long as the thumb; and perform another cautery outside the back, if you need to do so; and let these cauterizations be in the shape of a key according to the form described before.
de la marris	of the thigh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the thigh is cold and moist, and does not allow conception for that reason, and the flowers are corrupted and their terminations delayed; and when they come, there is great pain: then it must be done that three cauterizations are made around the buttocks, as we have said in the cautery of the bladder, and two cauterizations on the outside of the back; and let these cauterizations be key-shaped, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the thigh
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous fluids descend to the thigh joint, causing it to move from its place, and the sign of this is that one thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and if you find the source near there, then you must cauterize the patient on the thigh joint with a cautery resembling a circle, and mark in front of the area around the joint as it turns, so that the joint is within the circle; and let the cauterizations be like those used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if these cauterizations are not present, make three large olive oil cauterizations for him, and let the cauterizations be as deep as all other wounds; and treat until he is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain in the thigh
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the joint of the thigh, and it is due to coldness and moisture, and the patient is treated as we have described in the section but the treatment does not work, and the illness is old: then you must purge the patient of thick humors with foul-smelling pills or other similar good pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After you apply the cauterization; and the method of cauterization is in two ways: namely with burning medicines together, and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Cauterization with fire is done in many ways, one of which is as follows: you cauterize above the joint of the thigh three triangular cauteries according to this form, and make them deep and large, and there should be between each cautery a space the thickness of two fingers, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped; sometimes one makes a cautere in the middle at the top of the thigh, so there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you wish, cauterize with the circular cautery that we mentioned earlier for the dislocation of the thigh; but do it in such a way that the circles encompass the entire thigh, and all the ribs of the heart be burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done for sciatica, when the pain remains in the thigh and does not extend to the leg or the calf.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if it extends to the thigh and leg, place two cauteries where the patient says the pain is, and one above the ankle four fingers away; on the left side a little more. And let the cauteries be circular, or burn the thickness of the skin; and if the patient feels that the pain extends to three fingers or close to the instep, cauterize there where he feels the pain with a cautery called "three points" or "four points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if necessary, perform more; and if he knows that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, apply a cautery with the cutellaire or circular method, and take great care in all your cauterizations that you do not leave it so long as to burn the nerves and large arteries, and that you do not cause the patient greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who performed a cautery on the ankle of the foot, and they left it so long that the entire leg became swollen, and the foot as well, and it was pierced and corrupted throughout the whole foot.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a belly purge from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts at once, perform a cautery on each one according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the wise said in the cautery of the thigh, concerning which here is the manner, make it such iron and let it at the head be as thick as one new nail of oak, or a bit less, and let between the notches be and from one notch to the other of space the quantity of one knot of wood; and let the notches be covered on two sides, and let them also be like loops, and there should be one handle of iron well made; and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let it be heated until it is all red and sparks fly, and then place it on the side of the diseased thigh, and turn it towards the healthy side; and the cauterizer makes one cautery round and leaves it for three days; and then make a poultice of butter, and leave the wound uncovered for long; after the cure with ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasim says that we use this cautery little because of the fear of its appearance, and those who use it are few; yet this is one of the good cauteries, which whoever can endure finds beneficial.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The cautery instruments for burning medicine are such that you make them with interlocking parts in which the margin of the blade descends, and they should be made of brass or iron with one side long, and have two notches, with each notch having a width equal to the thickness of a finger; and let them be open at both ends and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After placing the thigh bone of the patient lying on their healthy side, and then place your hand much above the thigh bone; after that pour between the two circles of the heated awl which has been heated over fire for a little while, and leave it for one hour, allowing the patient to feel the heat and burning.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For there is a burning sensation as if from fire; and when the burning has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the thigh gently, and leave it thus for three days, and apply butter until the part that was blackened by the burn has peeled off; and let it be for three days so that pus may discharge; and this would be the last aid after the treatment of ointments until it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or to the leg, make an instrument that holds warm water as you did for the thigh similarly; and this is the way of using hot water, and I have written it in the treatise on the preparation of medicines.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkaline substances and quicklime, an equal amount of each, and grind them together, then put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	where there is a small opening for it to escape so that the point of a razor can enter; and place over that pot another well leaded pot, and put alkali and heat on top and let it have moisture until there are two layers of powder which you have properly prepared in your hand; and leave it thus until moisture and sediment come out of the leaded pot, then take all that moisture and pour it onto the alkali and heat as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And then it will be highly moistened and is administered in various works of medicine and in cauteries of other members Because it performs different work like fire, and there are other medicines with which one cauterizes the hip as well as testicle inflammation and honey anacardium and heat with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galien tells us of a cure where a nobleman was treated for hip pain and sciatic vein pain, and he praised it greatly, and said that no other treatment was done, and he was cured in one session when this treatment was performed, and he bathed as he instructs hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And he says in such a manner that you should take green and dry litharge and grind it much with a little grease, and apply it to the hip, thigh, and leg where the pain is present, and bind it; and leave it on for three hours until the patient no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then have him enter the bath until his body is somewhat refreshed, and then put him to bed, and the pain will go away completely and he will be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one must use a cautery of such medicines unless it is after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dioscorides stated that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat hair, it helps greatly; and the cauterization should be done in such a manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take wool and grease it with old oil, and place it on the hollow that is between the big toe of the foot and the other one called fuscule.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After that, take dry goat hair and hold it to the fire until it turns to embers, and place it on the wool, leaving it there until it is ashes; and do this again, and continue doing so until you think by sense that it reaches up to the thigh, and the pain is ceased; and this method of cauterization is called "goat hair cautery.
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or impact or due to excessive bloodletting, or from similar substances spread coldly, cauterization is not appropriate for any of these cases, except for one who suffers from an influx of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary after the patient has been treated with smelly pills or other similar treatments, to apply three lines of signs on the back where the pain is located, and in each line five cauterizations or more according to the strength and quantity that the patient can endure; and let the cauterizations be done according to the cautery which is called "poins"; and if you wish, make three cauterizations or four at the middle clavicle cautery according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This illness often comes to small children, and the signs of its beginning are that they have a tightness in the nape when they lie down, and fear; and you find it at the last vertebrae of the back and in the appearance which appears on the other vertebrae.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and wish to treat it, cauterize with the fire cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cautery affects each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you wish, cauterize around the spine with the piercing cautery in lines of two or three, and let the points be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treatment, ensure the area is healed as we have said, and beware of applying cauterization to a joint that is in a nerve cramp.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain in the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When joint pain is caused by fluids spread throughout each limb, and when the pain occurs in the feet, which doctors call "gout" properly, and when it is due to a cold cause and medicines cannot cure it, then it is treated with cauterizations in this manner: make several cauterizations around the joint of the foot, and let the cauterizations be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is need to cauterize the top of the foot, then make the cauterization as one calls it "point," the entire cauterization.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains come to the knees and other joints, which happens often, make a cautery on each knee three or four times on each part, for the whole cautery olive; and if you need more, do more, but hold your hand no further than until the thickness of the heart is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knee and the back, let the administrator apply the cautery that we have described in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are in the hands, make points around the wrist two lines; and if there remains pain in both, make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand; and if the pains come to the elbows or up to the shoulders, cauterize each part, and give good care to the patient and effective medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give it proper treatment and purge phlegm, he will be healed with God’s help.
de la routure dou syfac	of the fracture of the cheekbone
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When a fracture occurs in the jaws, and the teeth descend towards the genitals and this is newly happened, it must be that when you wish to treat him, he does not eat anything that day; and that he uses things which loosen the bowels so that his stool comes out of his body; afterwards make him sit on your lap between your hands, and command him to bite down firmly until the teeth are aligned, and realign them with your fingers, and cauterize from under the fracture above the bone of the little finger; then heat up the cautery which has this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	until they are white and shed flakes.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then reset the bones to their place; and the practitioner holds his hand over them so they do not move backward; and work well on the thighs of the patient, and put under him one cushion and another blanket over the thighs, and another under the buttocks which he holds with his hands; then apply the cautery to the mark with your whole hand, and hold it straight and keep it until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, repeat it again another time until you reach the bone; and be careful that the bone does not protrude when you perform the cautery; that you do not burn it; and by this, the patient does not die or suffer further harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And you should know that when you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that the cautery for children be subtle according to their size, and for adults as large as appropriate for them; after three days, treat the cauterized area with butter until the burn is gone; afterward, cure it with other ointments until it is healed, and have the patient lie on their back for forty days until the wound is well sealed; and it is necessary that their nourishment be given over a long period so that they do not strain their eyes when they are asked to go into rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise, provide him with a well-made bandage and have him wear it for another forty days; and let him rest properly, doing little work and being careful not to overeat or drink too much, and avoid raising his voice too loudly; and when he follows this instruction, he will be entirely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say hereafter the treatment for cutting in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures occur in other parts of the abdomen and are painful, and you wish to prevent them from growing further, apply the fire cautery according to its size, and let one-third be burned; afterward treat it as we have said; and some of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with a three-angled cautery in this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first mark the site and draw a line across the width above the rupture, and another below, and then proceed to make the entire cautery in this manner.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and gentler.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, whether from falling or being injured, and that pain lasts long, and medical treatment is ineffective, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called "points," and the cauterization should be according to the length of the limb and its smallness and weakness and strength and location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If he is healed by the first cauterization, it is good; if not, repeat another cauterization on that area, for such a custom is that it should change to the nearest limb, so you must perform the cauterizations until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	of confusion
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The ailments are sometimes aided by cautery with great care, especially the diseases that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	When you wish to cauterize, take care if the disease is in its beginning stages, and if it has progressed as we have described in the division, do not delay or hesitate, and if you fear that corruption may spread throughout the patient, then apply V cauteries on the head: I at the top of the head nine times, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the hair; II on the two temples, and I behind near the nape; and leave your hand such that the cauterizations reach to the bone, and until the skin comes out so that the vapors from thick humors can escape; and cauterize over the armpit as described before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And if the mischief is spread everywhere; and it shows clearly, then you must cauterize with those cauters that we have mentioned at the beginning, and one cautery on the nose, and two cauters on the neck vertebrae, and six cauters on the back vertebrae, and one large one on the buttocks and another nearby, and two on each shoulder; and two on the hips, and two on the tendons of the foot, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands; and beware of the nerves that are on the heel, so as not to burn them; and sometimes a person cauterizes on the bone of the wrist, and another on the bone of the stomach, and yet another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the more cauterizations you perform, the greater the help and benefit it provides; and know that the patient does not feel pain from the cautery as a healthy person would, because the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauteries be large and small according to the limbs and joints, as you will find them in the ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treating, apply flour of wheat with honey to the area and other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When swelling occurs in any limb and is treated with medicines, oils, and plasters, but it does not heal, then apply cauterizations on the limb according to its size; let them penetrate slightly into the thickness of the flesh; then treat with ointments until it heals.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And sometimes cautery is applied to the hand and foot and back, at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus the swelling is removed; yet one should not intervene with this if they are not knowledgeable about the limbs and the exits of the nerves moving the body.
de albaras	of alum
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the illness called "albaras" has taken hold and medicines are of no use, then cauterize with a hot cautery in a small spot according to the thickness of the skin, until the whiteness is removed and its color changes; then cure it with flour of vetches and lentils mixed with rose oil and plantain leaves, and one part each of dove's blood and lark's blood; mix all together, bind it with a cloth, and apply it to the affected area until it heals.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment of a boil by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a boil appears at the beginning and you wish to stop its development, then cauterize it with a ring-shaped cautery all around the edge of the boil.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And yet the wise say that one should make a cautery in the middle of the sore; and yet this does not seem good to me, for I fear it may become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have seen this happen some times; and more proper is it to cauterize around it, with the cautery called "circule," as we have said regarding many types of cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot be healed
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When someone has a disease called "adubelati," and it lingers due to the excess it causes, or due to the age of the patient when they are infirm (that is, too old), and there is little blood, or due to time; and you wish to hasten its end: then cauterize around with many small cauteries by pricking; after that, leave it as is.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will hurry to kill me.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you wish to pierce it with the entire cautery, then heat the cautery as follows:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of the disease called "adubelati" until the cautery has pierced the heart, and make the cautery such that the patient feels it from outside in such a way that the course of the putrefaction is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment until he is completely healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	the fire cautery with iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	There is another type of disease called "corrodens," and it is nothing other than a gnawing of the limb, for it eats away at the limbs as fire consumes dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in a place that can withstand cautery together with fire, then heat the cauterizing irons both small and large, according to what is needed for the location where the disease is; after that, cauterize all around until you reach all the corruption, and leave nothing of it, so that everything that is corrupted be removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then leave it for three days, and apply the treated areas with oil until the burns from the fire are removed, and all the corruption is gone.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment with ointments that generate flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that no healthy flesh is born, it is good; and if not, then restart the cauterization on what remains of the corrupted areas.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this meal was sometimes treated with a cold medicine instead of fire cautery; but still, the fire cautery is more helpful, and I have already said the treatment of the cold medicine in the section: take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	pains that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times a disease called "clos" according to our understanding arises in the feet from outside, and it is a swollen thing that impedes the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterizations for this disease are according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cauterization, and hot water cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	The fire cautery should be heated until it is as hot as a vulture's feather, and it should be made of good iron to the size that it can penetrate the nail from all sides, with fine edges; after heating it thoroughly on the fire, place it completely over the nail and move your hand around the nail until it reaches the bottom of the nail; leave it like this for III days until it begins to discharge pus; then make a poultice of wild mallow crushed with salt, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nail will fall out and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the area with an ointment that promotes flesh growth until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they are converted outward from the body, and this often happens in hands and feet, then you must apply hot water cautery to them; it is done as follows: take a chain of iron or steel, or a vulture's feather, and place it over the nail and althea leaves, which are known for removing warts; place the chain so that it surrounds everything, then pour some hot water on it, hold your hand firmly, and press your hand around so that the edge of the chain reaches the root of the nail, and the hot water can penetrate deeply to the root; allow the patient to suffer a little from the heat of the water for one hour; then leave it like this, and it will uproot itself entirely from its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Do this one after another, until you have examined all those who are on the body, then treat them with ointments that generate flesh.
li cure dou trembler	the treatment for trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When someone trembles from cold, nervousness, or quartan fever or another condition, you should perform IV cauterizations on the spine, one between each vertebra; and one on the feet, and one above the stomach at the olive cautery; this will stop the trembling and hasten recovery from the cold illness.
des pustules puans	the treatment for foul pus-filled blisters
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	At times, baths or foul pus-filled blisters appear on the surface of the body, which come from large corrupted substances.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	When they first appear, one should make a cauterization on each head of the pustule: a fine cauterization with a branch of myrtle, whose point is held over fire, or with a long root of artemisia, or a lentil-shaped cauterization.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And sometimes they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear, in this manner, and they cannot grow any further, but the excesses from which they come are broken, and they heal; but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Often there are great flows of blood from the artery that is cut at the wound coming from outside, or from incising an abscess, or from cauterizing a limb, and similar things; and it is very difficult to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And still when this happens to anyone, hasten to place your thumb on the wound of the vein, and press very hard until the blood is stilled under your thumb, and no more drops emerge; then put in the fire the olive cauteries several small and large until they are all red; then take one, either large or small according to the wound and the place where the artery runs, and place the cautery on that vein where you hold your thumb, and hold the cautery there until the blood is restrained.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it spurts out when you lift your thumb off the vein, and the cauteries are extinguished, then quickly take another of the cauteries that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not stop doing this one after another until the blood is restrained; and be careful that you do not burn the nerve which is nearby, and that no other harm comes to the patient; and know that when blood spurts from an artery, it cannot be properly staunched by itself when the artery is large, unless it is done in one of the four ways we have said: either by cautery, or extraction if it has not yet been treated, or by tightly binding with thread, or by applying medicines which have the power to restrain blood; and bind and press firmly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will attend to the removal of stench by tightly covering with cloths or placing burning substances upon it, or other similar things, if there is no benefit from doing so.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and there is no physician or medicine present, then he should place his thumb on the wound of the vein as we have said, and extend it well until it becomes cold over the wound and over the vein; and do not move it, but wet it with very cold water often so that the blood coagulates and thickens and clots; and make him do this before those who need cautery and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of treatments for wounds
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have told you in the first chapter about every disease in which fire cautery or hot medicine is required, and the questions, causes, instruments, and forms of the cauterizations; and I placed that chapter from head to foot, and I will proceed in this chapter along the same path so that one finds more easily what one seeks.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And thus as I begin this, it is necessary, dear scribe, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear regarding cauteries than in the first chapter, and for that reason greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you that you do not undertake folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many kinds of people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	They come from those who are so afflicted by their illness that they change easily due to the madness they find in their sickness, and from the severity of their condition; one must be afraid of such people.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And among these, there are those who regain their senses and say: "Wait, I am cured"; yet the illness is severe.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	It is not fitting that you agree with those who come to you in this manner, but place more importance on your honor than on your desire, and do not act foolishly but wisely regarding those about whom you are certain and from whom you can gain respect and praise; and use prognosis and indications in the treatment of your patients for whom health should be restored; and this will help you acquire a good reputation, glory, and commendation.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Most gracious Lord, Our Lords grant you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to inspire from the holy inspiration of His hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Now I have ordered this chapter by dividing it into sections, according to what is before the chapter on cauterizations, which I have described from head to foot, so that you may more easily find what you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	the head full of fluid
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	Know that this disease often comes to children at birth, and when the head of the child is held too tightly; and sometimes it happens for reasons that are not known.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I have never seen this disease except in children, and in all those whom I have seen it hastened death; and for this reason, it seems to me that I should leave off working on such cases.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I saw the child whose head was full of water, and his head swelled each day until he could no longer hold it up; and the moisture grew so much that he died, and this moisture is gathered below the bone on the siphon, between the heart and the bone; and if the work is such that the moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscess is small, then you should cut a wide fissure in the head; and make it as long as two fingers, until the moisture flows; and see here the form of the spatumile:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more abundant, and the abscess is larger, then make two cuts in the shape of a cross, following this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the moisture is below the bone, and you see the creases of the head open on each side, and the fluid jumps out when you press it with your hand from inside, and there is no response: then you must cut three fissures in the head according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all the moisture thoroughly.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After extracting the crevices of cloths and powders, and place wine and oil, and leave it thus until the fifth day; then untie it, and treat the wound with bandages and ointments, and let the head drain evenly, and give the patient dried meat with little moisture until the limb is healed and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way of incision is to look where the swelling of the abscess is most prominent and the collection of fluid; for sometimes it is in front; sometimes behind; sometimes on the right; and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Cut there where the abscess is most prominent and the fluid accumulation, and make the incision according to what you can do; and be careful not to cut the artery; and if blood flows, it may cause the patient to die from loss of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of phlegm
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When someone falls ill with a disease called "cataract" in the eyes or forehead, and the illness is old, and medical treatment does no good, then the final remedy is cauterization using what will cut the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Therefore, when you cut the veins, the patient should lie on his back; then rub the area with a rough cloth until the arteries become visible, then stretch the patient's neck against the entire cloth; then look where the vein runs, and their locations are behind the ears, and are placed there; then mark the spots, then cut each one with a sharp spatumile from both sides, until the veins reach the bone, and this should be done along the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you wish, place the spatula under the artery and the cloth above, cutting as you must through it.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, the blood will continuously spurt out forcefully.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And if the artery does not open upon feeling it, you must measure a distance of three fingers, then cut through to the bone; and the amount of blood that should be let out is six cups, and perhaps more or less depending on what the patient can tolerate, and the fullness of the artery; then examine the wound: if there remains any soft tissue on the bone, cut it away so no harmful abscesses form, then press and bandage the wound, and treat with ointment until it heals.
de emigrainne	of migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an old migraine comes with acute catarrh, due to the moisture of tears and heat in the temples and a long-standing insane sore and similar things, and it is treated by medical methods and remedies but nothing helps, then we extract the arteries from the temples and apply cautery as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method of extracting them is that the patient shaves the hair from their temples and listens to the artery which can be heard in the temple, as it beats clearly, though it may not be audible in some people who are too cold; if it is audible, then the patient should press on its side with some cloths, then rub the area with a rough cloth, and rinse the area with hot water until the artery appears clearly; then take the spatumile of which here is the form:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	Then scrape the skin lightly until you reach the artery, then trace it upwards to the ligatures, and separate it well from the tissues that are beneath each part; and if the artery is fine, turn it with the tip of the hook, then cut it according to the quantity of the two heads.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, then the blood will not flow out completely.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And draw out the blood from six fingers' width up to three; and if the artery is large, tie it with a double silk thread in two places so that no corruption comes before the healing of the wound and prevent further bleeding; then cut off the excess between the two ties at that same moment, and then, if you wish, apply the cautery from the cautery knife to the bone until the heads are cut off; this is the main work, provided the patient does not have a fever and has a warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For the cauterizes are helpful to finish the treatments: for this reason, they are of greater aid in treating moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	For when it is necessary to extract arteries, one should fill the area with old cotton and place well-made tents on top; and when they are unwrapped, treat them with dry medicines that promote flesh growth and use tents until healing occurs; and if there is no cort of the artery as you work, hasten to cut by cautery, filling the space with vitriol and holding it in your hand so that the skin contracts; and if you do not have this available, place your own paste on the area until the skin is frozen, and rinse the area with cold water until the skin ceases to contract, and hold it as required; and what is milder and quicker in extracting arteries is that you cauterize the vein of this cautery cutting from two sides, but ensure the cuts are well-spaced to preserve their heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instrument is too cold, it holds less of its heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus; et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And there should be one thick space between the two knives, and then when you have marked the two places with a pin, place the hot iron on it until it reaches the bone, and cut the vein in two places; and keep them apart between the two points because they are not joined together by this cautery throughout; and this is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the tears from the eyes come down from the veins that are above the forehead of fire, and it does no good with any medicine you apply, and you see the face of the patient turn red, and feel on the forehead shaking as if trembling; and when the eyes are cold and moist so that the hair on the cheeks falls out, and the cheeks are heated and scorched by the heat of the tears, then there is need for this treatment.
